# `n`           a positive integer
# `factorzig`   the prime factors of n, indented by distance from the nearest prime
# `hsum`        the harmonic sum, the sum of the reciprocals of the prime factors of n
# `pi`          the prime counting function π(n), the number of primes less than or equal to n
# `piest`       an estimate of the prime counting function π(n), the number of primes less than or equal to n: n / (log n - 1)
# `riemannr`    the Riemann R function R(n)
# `riemannli`   the logarithmic integral Li(n)
# `cheby`       the Chebyshev θ(n) function, the sum of log p for primes p ≤ n
# `chebypow`    the Chebyshev ψ(n) function, the sum of log p for prime powers p^k ≤ n
# `vonmangoldt` the von Mangoldt function of n, Λ(n)
# `numdiv`      the number of divisors of n, τ(n)
# `sumdiv`      the sum of divisors of n, σ(n)
# `eulertot`    the Euler totient of n, φ(n)
# `carmichael`  the Carmichael function of n, λ(n)
# `dedekind`    the Dedekind ψ(n) function
# `mob`         the Möbius function of n, which is 1 if n is a product of an even number of distinct primes, -1 if odd, and 0 if any prime is repeated
# `numfacs`     the number of distinct prime factors of n, ω(n)
# `totfacs`     the total number of prime factors of n, counting multiplicity, Ω(n)
# `liouville`   the Liouville function of n, λ(n) = (-1)^Ω(n)
# `mertens`     the Mertens function M(n)
# `m*`          the prime residues of n modulo a set of primes
# `psym`        the symmetric primes at equal offsets around n
# `rad`         the radical of n, the product of its unique prime factors
# `mask`        the mask of prime factors (radical) of n, as a string
